Et quant il est desaluez dou tot, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et le tigne I ministres fors par la jambe, desus la cheville; puis trai le piet a toi a ta main destre, et puis a la senestre II fois, puis l’estent en haut, et boute bellement lou piet en haut; et fai ce II fois, si com nos avons dit, em boutant et en traiant lou piet; s’elle revient, c’est bien; se ce non, si rencomence l’ovraige, car il revient; et s’il ne puet revenir ensi, si fai gesir lou malaide sor son dos sus terre, et fiche I passeil fermement en terre entre ses cuixes, et lie drapelz entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide; puis teigne li ministres la cuixe, et uns autres ministres estende lou piet a ses mains ou a I liien, k’il lie sus le col dou piet; puis estende chescuns ministres igalment, et li passelz soit adés entre les cuixes dou malaide por retenir le malaide quant on l’estent; puis mette li mires igal la dislocation a ses mains, et uns autres ministres teigne la jambe sainne au desoz, et li dislocation revenra hastanment.	And when it is fully dislocated, you must seat the patient upright, and have one assistant firmly grasp the leg above the ankle; then pull the foot towards you with your right hand, and then with your left hand two times, then extend it upwards, and gently push the foot upwards; do this twice, as we have said, by pushing and pulling the foot; if it returns, that is good; if not, repeat the procedure, for it will return; and if it cannot be returned thus, have the patient lie on their back on the ground, place one peg firmly in the ground between their thighs, and tie a cloth around it so as not to injure the patient; then have an assistant hold the thigh, and another extend the foot by hand or with a rope tied above the ankle; then each assistant extends equally, and the peg is placed between the patient’s thighs to hold them down when they are being extended; then the doctor places the dislocation back in position with their hands, and another assistant holds the healthy leg below, and the dislocation will return quickly.
Et quant elle iert a point, si met l’emplastre et estoupes sus, et l’estrain forment, et lie lou piet a la jambe, et warde les ners qui sont sus la cheville derrier, que li liiens ne soit trop estrois; puis le laisse II jors ou III, et se li liiens amolist, si l’estrain; puis le deslie au tier jor ou au quart, et deffent a aler lou malaide par IIII jors; et s’il va devant cel termine, ce n’est mie seurtez qu’il ne desalue encor.	And when it is ready, then place the plaster and bandages on, and bind tightly, and tie the foot to the leg, and watch the nerves that are above the ankle behind, so that the binding is not too tight; then leave it for two days or three, and if the binding softens, then bind again; then untie it on the third day or fourth, and forbid the patient to walk for four days; and if he walks before this time, it is not certain that it will not dislocate again.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si covient que tu l’apaises, si com nos avons dit autre part, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if hot abscesses come, then you must soothe it, as we have said elsewhere, until it is healed.
des dois	of the two
Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.	When both are dislocated, then they must be gently extended without effort, and this is an easy thing to do.
Et se li dislocations est en aucun nout dou dos dou piet, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide sus I leu plain ou sus .ie. table tot droit, et met ton piet sus ce qui apert de ces jointures, puis presse a ton piet forment, tant qu’il reviegne; et quant il est igalz, et il n’i apert nient, si met desoz la plante dou piet une table a II chiés, puis l’estrain forment, et le laisse III jors, puis le deslie; et le fai reposer, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the dislocation is in any joint of the back of the foot, then you must make the patient sit on a flat place or on a table straight up, and put your foot on what appears of these joints, then press hard with your foot until it returns; and when it is evened out, and nothing shows, then place under the sole of the foot a board with two feet, then pull hard, and leave it for three days, then untie it; and have it rest until it is healed.
de plaie et de dislocation ensamble	of wound and dislocation together
Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert: si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis; et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit; et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne; et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis; et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples; et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors.	When a wound comes with the dislocation, and you wish to restore it, often the patient dies: so be not presumptuous in the treatment, if you are not wise in the art and have not long practiced it, and if you are not pitying and merciful and cautious, not bold; and use at first things that calm a hot abscess, and leave the patient in God’s hands if you see no hope of health; and when you see hope, then reset now the limb to its place, although the hot abscess comes; and when the limb is in place, then administer things that calm a hot abscess, and treat the wound as it should be with drying ointments; and if there is also a fracture with the dislocation, and small bones disjointed, then remove them, and do what we have said in simple diseases; and beware of entering the way of fear according to what I have said, for this profits you nothing according to your Creator, and for the wisdom of your arm and body.
Amen	Amen
